***majesteitsschennis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:majesteitsschennis.html>majesteitsschennis</a> (103328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:majesteit.html>majesteit</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schennis.html>schennis</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:majesteitsschennis.html>majesteitsschennis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:majesteitsschennis.html>majesteitsschennissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:majesteitsschennis.html>majesteitsschennisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lese majesty, high crime against the person of a monarch, or the monarchy or crown; by extension <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> against any sovereign state (which in Roman law <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the original holder of 'majesty', only <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> a ruler's title)</li></ol>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">knapenschennis</span></li></ul>

***maken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a> (141)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:macon.html>macon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*makōn</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fix, to repair, to mend</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take (a photo)</li></ol>

***makken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> (40537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bargoens" class="extiw" title="w:Bargoens">Bargoens</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spend money
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allure.html>allure</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:welgesteld.html>welgesteld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezin.html>gezin</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigenlijk.html>eigenlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> cent <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:airs.html>airs</a> of a well-to-do family, but actually <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not have a cent to <b>spend</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Only found in the expressions <i><a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> ("have nothing to spend") or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> cent <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a></i> ("have not [<a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a>] a cent to spend").</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:makken.html>makken</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">macker</i>, probably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*gemacke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a> (5452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallen.html>mallen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>malletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mold, cast <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device to help creating shapes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>maller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">malst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foolish, crazy, lacking common sense</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mal.html>mal</a></i> always refers to an aspect of a thing or person. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the adjective form of the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallerd.html>mallerd</a></i>. For other senses, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dwaas.html>dwaas</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dom.html>dom</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a></i> are used.
</p>

***malaise.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a> (68874)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Latn headword" lang="id">malaisê</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">depression</span>, a period of major economic contraction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a></span>, a feeling of general bodily discomfort, fatigue or unpleasantness, often at the onset of illness.</li></ol>

***malen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a> (8055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mālen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*malan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*malan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*malaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to grind</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">mâlen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*mālon</i>, denominative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*māl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spot, stain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maal.html>maal</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:malen.html>malen</a></strong>
</p>

***mallard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mallard.html>mallard</a> (90925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">malarde</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">mawdelare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">malart</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mallart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild duck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly derived from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">Madelhart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">proper name</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">whence the English forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">maudelard</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mawdelard</i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; or alternatively from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">male</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:malle.html>malle</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">male</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ard</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallard.html>mallard</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mallards</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:mallard.html>mallard</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A common and widespread dabbling duck, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:anas.html>Anas</a> platyrhynchos</i>, whose male <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a distinctive dark green head.</li></ol>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*molko-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leather bag</span><span <p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">malot</i>, a dialectal word for a horsefly or gadfly.

<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mamba.html>mamba</a></i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Afrikaans" class="extiw" title="w:Afrikaans"><a href = vnd.unilang:afrikaans.html>Afrikaans</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="af"><a href = vnd.unilang:mamba.html>mamba</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zulu_language" class="extiw" title="w:Zulu language"><a href = vnd.unilang:zulu.html>Zulu</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zu">imamba</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swazi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swazi language">Swazi</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mamba.html>mamba</a></i>.

***man.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> (102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mann-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mans.html>mans</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mannetje.html>mannetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manneke.html>manneke</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">manneken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></a>, human male, either <a href = vnd.unilang:adult.html>adult</a> or age-irrespective
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>zee</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/en:The_Old_Man_and_the_Sea" class="extiw" title="w:en:The Old Man and the Sea">The Old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></b> and the Sea</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>husband, male spouse</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The normal plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>mannen</a></i>. The unchanged form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used after numerals only; it refers to the size of a group rather than a number of individuals. For example: <i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:totaal.html>totaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verloren.html>verloren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> 5000 <u><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></u> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slag.html>slag</a>.</i> (“5000 <u><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></u> altogether <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> their <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> in that battle.”) The plural <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mans.html>mans</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> dated, now mostly occurring in nautical contexts or in dialect.</li>
<li>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> with <i>-man</i> as their last component often take <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lieden.html>lieden</a></i> or <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lui.html>lui</a></i> in the plural, rather than <i>-mannen</i>. For example: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerman.html>brandweerman</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">firefighter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> → <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerlieden.html>brandweerlieden</a></i> (alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweerlui.html>brandweerlui</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandweermannen.html>brandweermannen</a></i>).</li>
<li>Various alternative diminutives exist, including <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manneke.html>manneke</a></i> (used especially in Flanders) and the dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mannechie</i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a></span></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:biologie.html>biologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mannelijk.html>mannelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geslacht.html>geslacht</a>

***mandarijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijn.html>mandarijn</a> (27553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">mandarim</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">menteri</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms">manteri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">मन्त्रि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mantri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">मन्त्रिन्</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mantrin</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">minister, councillor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijn.html>mandarijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijnen.html>mandarijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijntje.html>mandarijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A mandarin, Far Eastern (notably Chinese Imperial) high official</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A pundit, someone in/with authority
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijnen.html>mandarijnen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:schaden.html>schaadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reputatie.html>reputatie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brui.html>brui</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>pundits</b> ruined his reputation so badly he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to call it quits.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">mandarine</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijn.html>mandarijn</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijnen.html>mandarijnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandarijntje.html>mandarijntje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">often in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:tangerine.html>tangerine</a>, a mandarin orange, an orange-like fruit.</li></ol>

</p>

***mandrake.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a> (27048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">mandragora</i>, with <i>-dragora</i> reinterpreted as related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dragon</i> and replaced with native <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>drake</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mandrakes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mythology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mandragora, a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of tiny <a href = vnd.unilang:demon.html>demon</a> immune to fire.</li>
<li>Any plant of the genus <i>Mandragora</i>, certain of which are <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to have medicinal properties; the root of these plants often resembles the shape of a small person, hence occasioning various mythic, magical, or occult uses.</li>
<li>A root of a <a href = vnd.unilang:mandrake.html>mandrake</a> plant that resembled human form, especially one kept or used for magic or occult purposes.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1936</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:rollo.html>Rollo</a> Ahmed,  <cite>The Black Art</cite>, London |  Long, page 75:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>Mandrakes</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> sometimes considered in the light of familiars. Witches kept both male and female <a href = vnd.unilang:specimens.html>specimens</a> of the magic root in bottles[.]</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The drug methaqualone.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mandies</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mandragora</span></li></ul>
</body>

***mangaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mangaan.html>mangaan</a> (103308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:maniac.html>maniac</a> (68862)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">maniaque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">maniacus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μανιακός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maniakós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, adjectival form of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μανία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">madness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:maniac.html>maniac</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">maniacs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An insane person, especially one who <a href = vnd.unilang:suf.html>suffers</a> from a mania.</li>
<li>A fanatic, a person with an obsession.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">madling</span></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">-maniac</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">mania</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">maniacal</span></li></ul>
